  <script>
   function getOneSignalUserID() {
    var oneSignalUserIDStr = window.localStorage && window.localStorage.getItem("oneSignalUserID");
    var oneSignalUserID = oneSignalUserIDStr && oneSignalUserIDStr !== "null"
      ? oneSignalUserIDStr
      : undefined;

    return oneSignalUserID;
  }

  function trackOneSignalUserId(oneSignalUserID) {
    if (!oneSignalUserID) return;

    window.dataLayer.push({
      event: "oneSignalUpdate",
      eventCategory: "PushNotifications",
      eventAction: "UpdateOneSignalID",
      eventLabel: oneSignalUserID,
      one_signal_userID: oneSignalUserID
    });
  }

  // Set custom dimension before pageview tracking
  trackOneSignalUserId(getOneSignalUserID());
  </script>
